< text>
Just finished dinner here with some great sashimi, sushi rolls and sparkling sake. This place seems to working very hard to build an ongoing clientele, and their efforts made me want to help by sharing my experience. Their secret strategy appears to include great food, large portions, reasonable prices and lavish attention on the customer.  Seriously, the service and attention we received was well above your average night out and the 8 piece sashimi combo with 2 sushi rolls was fantastic with generous portions. My wife and my sister ordered a couple of tasty rolls and appetizers and we shared what turned out to be too much food. We enjoyed all we could eat and boxed tomorrow‚Äôs lunch with the rest. Walked away with a new favorite place in the valley.</text>

< review>
The old man that runs this donut shop is the nicest business owner ever. He's always chatting up his customers, giving away free donuts, or just beaming a smile.

My family and I come to this shop not just because it's the closest shop to our home but honestly because the taste is fantastic here and the customer service can't be beat compared to every other donut shop in the area.

Donuts here are fresh and not too sweet or tasteless. The dough is always fluffy and the icing on the donuts are perfect. Other places taste kind of fake and leave a waxy texture coating the roof of your mouth but these donuts are always great. I've never had a bad one here. Honestly the best donut shop in Stockton.

The shop is a little older but it's always clean. I'm not sure what happened to the other reviewer who said it was dirty but as a clean freak, I've never felt grossed out here. It's just an older establishment, but the shop itself is really clean.</review>

< Review>
Fine place, fine people, well organized. The stock is rotated regularly, so you don't wind up with old expired product. They have loyalty cards, specials, good online service, great selection AND are prompt at getting special orders in stock. Their pricesare competitive with even the big-box stores. I find that if you need specific knowledge about product and technique it's best to go weekdays during business hours and to find one of the more experienced employees....there are one or two in particular at my locale who are VERY knowledgeable. They respect the customer's needs and their pocketbook. I have NEVER had anything less than a good experience, and they've never sent me away with more than I need.< /Review>
